"Pieris rapae","2005-06-07 14:04:00 -0400","I saw this butterfly flying, but it looked a little funny.  Turned out it was 2 butterflies!  There was only one flapping its wings; the other was just along for the ride.  Maybe they had different ideas about whether they wanted to go somewhere or not. :-)  Or maybe going somewhere only works if 1 does the flying for both!  Got this shot when they set down.  Wingspan ~ 5 cm.

This is the Cabbage White, one of only 2 nonnative butterfly species in New Jersey.  Unfortunately, it seems to be the most common butterfly, at least around human habitation.
